   <h1 class="title">
    <a href="http://tradesportsinsider.com/top-8-richest-players-in-2014-world-cup/" rel="bookmark" title="Permalink to Top 8 Richest Players In 2014 World Cup">
     Top 8 Richest Players In 2014 World Cup
    </a>
   </h1>
   <div class="post-meta">
    <ul>
     <li class="date">
      June 17, 2014 at 4:15 pm
     </li>
     <li class="author">
      by
      <a href="http://tradesportsinsider.com/author/tsinsideradmin/" rel="author" title="Posts by Dan Karpuc">
       Dan Karpuc
      </a>
     </li>
     <li class="category">
      in

   <section id="main" role="main">
    <div class="clearfix post-2849 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-uncategorized" id="post-2849">
     <div class="entry">
      <p>
       If the World Cup obsession has hit you as well, youll appreciate seeing which players have accrued the most money in their careers and who have the most net worth. Below are the top 8 wealthiest players in this years World Cup, according to a
       <strong>
        <span style="color: #ff0000;">
         <em>
          <a href="http://www.wealthx.com/articles/2014/top-10-richest-world-cup-2014-players/" target="_blank">
           <span style="color: #ff0000;">
            Wealth-X report
           </span>
          </a>
         </em>
        </span>
       </strong>
       .
      </p>
      <h3>
       8. Steven Gerrard ($55 Million Net Worth)
      </h3>
      <p>
       <iframe allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen" frameborder="0" height="360" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/3offv9FL79Y" width="640">
       </iframe>
      </p>
      <h3>
       7. Frank Lampard, England ($60 Million Net Worth)
      </h3>
      <p>
       <iframe allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen" frameborder="0" height="360" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/e6bXlI1-HNk" width="640">
       </iframe>
      </p>
      <h3>
       6. Yaya Toure, Ivory Coast ($70 Million Net Worth)
      </h3>
      <p>
       <iframe allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen" frameborder="0" height="360" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/qbX09lyJhbM" width="640">
       </iframe>
      </p>
      <h3>
       5. Samuel Etoo, Cameroon ($75 Million Net Worth)
      </h3>
      <p>
       <iframe allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen" frameborder="0" height="360" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/lKS8wl4S_Gs" width="640">
       </iframe>
      </p>
      <h3>
       4. Didier Drogba, Ivory Coast ($90 Million Net Worth)
      </h3>
      <p>
       <iframe allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen" frameborder="0" height="360" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/bn-SekWHpuA" width="640">
       </iframe>
      </p>
      <h3>
       3. Wayne Rooney, England ($95 Million Net Worth)
      </h3>
      <p>
       <iframe allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen" frameborder="0" height="360" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/2mDNQ_UsAl8" width="640">
       </iframe>
      </p>
      <h3>
       2. Lionel Messi, Argentina ($180 Million Net Worth)
      </h3>
      <p>
       <iframe allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen" frameborder="0" height="360" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/qIGJNlpI5XU" width="640">
       </iframe>
      </p>
      <h3>
       1. Cristiano Ronaldo, Portugal ($230 Million Net Worth)
      </h3>
      <p>
       <iframe allowfullscreen="allowfullscreen" frameborder="0" height="360" src="//www.youtube.com/embed/7ThHAz8YS74" width="640">
       </iframe>
      </p>
      <h4>
       <span style="color: #ff0000;">
        Enjoy watching all of the above superstar players on the pitch during the World Cup and be sure to
        <span style="text-decoration: underline;">
         <strong>
          <a href="http://www.tradesports.com" target="_blank">
           SIGN UP HERE
          </a>
         </strong>
        </span>
        to play daily fantasy World Cup trading contests on Tradesports.com, where you trade sports like stocks!
       </span>
      </h4>

		function createParamsString(paramsAsObj) {
			var params = [];
			for (var key in paramsAsObj) {
				if (paramsAsObj.hasOwnProperty(key)) {
					params.push(key + "=" + paramsAsObj[key]);
				}
			}
			return params.join("&amp;");
		}

		function appendTradesportsUrl(urlId) {
			var thisUrlHasParams = false,
					gaParamsKey = "ts.insider.ga.params",
					tradesportsLinkEl = jQuery("." + urlId).children("a")[0],
					params;

			var gaParamsObj = function () {
				var str = window.location.search;
				var objURL = {};
				str.replace(
						new RegExp("([^?=&amp;]+)(=([^&amp;]*))?", "g"),
						function ($0, $1, $2, $3) {
							if ($1.indexOf("utm_") == 0) {
								objURL[ $1 ] = $3;
								thisUrlHasParams = true;
							}
						}
				);
				return objURL;
			}();

			if (thisUrlHasParams) {
				params = createParamsString(gaParamsObj);
				localStorage.setItem(gaParamsKey, params);
			} else {
				params = localStorage.getItem(gaParamsKey) || "";
			}

			if (params) {
				tradesportsLinkEl.href = tradesportsLinkEl.href + "?" + params;
			}
		}

		jQuery(appendTradesportsUrl("tradesports-link"));
